< Review>
Super cute cafe! I was definitely impressed by the place. I heard so much about their cloud drinks that I had to try one out for myself. The place did not disappoint.  Good walking distance from all the restaurants in downtown Pasadena. It has lots of open seating and the staff is very attentive.  They also have samples to try when we came in.  Audrey was very helpful in introducing me to the teas they used and helped us with our selection.

I got their Fresh Strawberry Cloudy drink because it looked so tasty and pretty.  My hubby got a Jasmine Chappuccino. I really liked that their foam was avocado based in my Fresh Strawberry Cloudy drink. It is completely different from other cafes and tastes really good!  Hubby liked his drink too; light jasmine with light foam on top.  They have a small assortment of pastries too.  We bought the egg tart and it was a good amount of sweetness.  Yummy!

The decor is simple yet elegant.  I will be back to try the other flavors!</Review>

< text>
My favorite coffee chain from the Bay is finally making its way into LA! They blend and roast their own beans. For hot coffee, i recommend Ambrosia Coffee of God‚Äîdark, rich, complex. For iced coffees, you can't go wrong with either the Mint Mojito or the Gingersnap. They'll ask if you want it the "house way," or you can specify how much cream and sweetener you prefer. Personally, I leave it to the capable experts behind the counter.

Downsides for this location include difficult parking in the neighborhood (Philz validates for 30 min; otherwise, metered street parking) and loud music (tough if you want to study or work).

Free Wi-Fi.< /text>

< Review>
Its been a little over a week and the car looks amazing! No bubbles and no imperfections have been spotted. So uniform and finally its glare-free inside (I don't understand people who can drive without tinted windows in Southern California). I can't stand not having some protection from the ridiculously intense glare and Retina-piercing sun when driving the I-15 cajon pass around 4-5pm when the sun is at low angle. I am very happy with their work!

After asking around and reading reviews I chose to walk in and check this place out. I needed my new BMW 330i tinted and I was definitely pretty weary and untrusting of basically all the places I called in the High Desert and l.E.

I spoke with Eric and Ashley and was convinced that they were knowledgeable and professional enough to handle the Bimmer. They have computer cut patterns for accuracy and use 3M films which is what all of my friends recommended. I chose to get the 3M Color Stable series 20% all around!

Next step is to go in and get some 3M Crystalline for my front windshield.</Review>

< Text>
I had my window tint done by DeluxeAuto Sport after I moved out the the High Desert. I drive a BMW so naturally I don't let just anyone work on my car. They walked me through the different prices and the pros and cons of each type of tint, the warranties and helped me make the right decision. I left the car with them and when I got it back, the tint looked so perfect. The windows on my car are difficult to tint due to the fact that they sit under the window trim and lower when you open the door which usually leaves tint shops leaving a small gap at the top of the window, not DeluxeAuto Sport. They made sure to tint the windows from top to bottom all the way around. After I received my car, they walked me around and made sure that it was too my satisfaction and explained the care procedures to me.

DeluxeAuto Sport is the kind of shop that I would recommend and have recommended to any and all car enthusiasts or even just someone looking for a basic tint job. I know I will be returning to get my rear window tinted after having the last one replaced.<//Text>

< Review>
This is a Korean fusion eatery, serving all sorts kind of interesting food that you don't usually find in regular Korean restaurants.

I went here while looking for kimbab. Ordered a few rolls, and must say wasn't too impressed. But the other day I tried ordering the Seoul burger and sweet potato fries, now those were pretty good. Beef patty, bulgogi beef, egg inside of a burger bun, served with the sweet potato fries (which is just okay), pretty good food.

All in all, if you're bored with regular Korean restaurants, you can try the food in here. The also serve larvae, which I don't event think of trying. But hey maybe some of you are adventurous enough? :)< /Review>

< user_id>
114714540192669718999</user_id>
<username>B. Li< /username>< date>
1565576457377<//date>
<Rating>4<//Rating><review>[updated]
Still a good late night spot, particularly for burgers and sides, good service that checks up on you to make sure things are OK. But when I come back, I'm probably not going to get the donkatsu again.

Donkatsu itself was fine, but small issues with the sides added up to a disappointing dish.

Came with 3 small sides, japchae (plain japchae, no veggies mixed in), chilled daikon and carrot slices, and beansprouts. A little disappointed that the japchae was plain as it's the small things like the green onions and chopped onions that make it more than just plain carbs. Chilled daikon and carrot slices go well with donkatsu since it can cleanse your palate.

The bean sprouts were entirely disappointing. It was plain chilled bean sprouts, just taken from a container. As such, it was watery; the plate was in a concave form, so the water from the flavorless bean sprouts flowed down and met the bottom crumbs of the donkatsu, leaving a soggy texture and watered down flavor. The beansprouts themselves could've been easily improved with a drizzle of sesame oil and pepper.

Last small note would be that I was only given a fork, no accompanying knife. Minor issue as I could've just asked or gotten one myself, just odd that they didn't include it. Obviously, one of the donkatsu slices wasn't cut through, and eating the last bits of the side dishes was troublesome as there isn't a utensil to stabilize the side dishes.

I'll come back at some point, but the donkatsu is a decent dish that's held down by the side dishes and I cannot recommend it for anyone who has an itch for it.
[/updated]

Solid sweet potato fries

Bulgogi rice entree was large and easily fills you up. The sauce is lighter than most other Korean places, but the flavors are there and works well.

Seoul burger is 50% of the reason I come here. It's a mess to eat, but it's got everything I want in a burger from the egg to the sauce.</review><pics>None<//pics>< resp>

This place is good!  I really really enjoyed myself here when I stopped in after some errands in Hillcrest.  The sandwiches were so unique and the bread some of the freshest I've had in some time!  I got The Illusionist, which I was told would be spicy and although I didn't find it very spicy it was VERY good!  They also carry soup which in my mind is so hard to find!  I didn't get any but, asked which soups she had that day and I was told Chicken and Dumpling, second choice being Mushroom Brie.  Both sound out of this world!  The french bread was some of the best I've had in awhile, it wasn't too hard on the outside but, had a good crust and it was easy to bite.  I can't wait next time that I'm in Hillcrest for lunch and in the mood for a sandwich I will heavily consider stopping in here again! Cool dessert.. order on your own on their iPads. The program takes you step by step through the process of ordering. < Review>
This place is very busy and hectic, with the dessert pickup not exactly having a great setup to wait for your dessert or ensure you get the right one. But that was my only issue with the place. The desserts are pricey, but lots of fun and tasty. The Vegas Bowl is just placing your dessert in a bowl with dry ice- great for pics or kids, but no other added value. <userid>117416368577181681778<//userid>< text>
The wife brought me here for our date night.  The place was pretty awesome.  I'm not one for upscale dessert places but it was cool to place an order and pay on the iPads and then grab a seat. < text>
I highly recommend this place! The concept was great! The staff was very friendly and the place looks so chic and very pleasing to the eyes! Boyfriend chose this place when we were looking for a dessert place. I didn‚Äôt know what this place is or what it was offering, until we arrive! And my gosh! As soon as we walked in, I feel in love with the place! ‚ù§Ô∏è

There was not a lot of people when we went here as it was raining. There were actually only two couples inside. We went to the front because my boyfriend and I were clueless on how everything works, the staff at the register explained everything well. We chose to customize our own dessert so we went to one of the iPads on the wall. We chose meringue because this is what they are really known for! They offer a lot more kind of desserts like cakes, shakes, etc.! But my boyfriend and I wanted to try the meringue. They have 16 different meringues, all were handcrafted and looks so pretty! The customization process on the iPad was so easy to go through, it was user friendly. You can always go back to the previous step if you want to change something on your order before submitting it! After submitting our order and paying it on the iPad, the staff at the front had immediately started making our customized meringue!

The wait time for our meringue was not that bad, I think we waited for like 6-7 minutes before we were called. When we finally got our order, my boyfriend and I were both excited for it! The taste was heavenly! It was so good! We both enjoyed it so much! The dessert is not only pretty, it was also delicious!<//text>

< name>
Lorie Lacasa< /name>
< Date>
1479506282718</Date>
< rate>
5< /rate>
< text>
I found out about this place just walking through little italy. I remember being drawn in by their interior design and unusually placed ipads at the counter. There was a case on the wall that was filled with these round things (crust), so I wanted to see what it was all about.

I built my own dessert. It's an innovative dessert concept- you pick a crust (16+ to choose from), and pick a gelato/sorbet to go in it. You also get to pick a cake (5 flavors), and a cream, sauce or fruit to go with it. If you want to be extra fancy, you can get the vegas bowl to have that dry ice effect in the photos.

I went with a coffee crust, mocha gelato, spiced vanilla cream, vanilla cake and some caramel sauce. Clearly I was going for a coffee/chai kind of dessert, but I loved it! The vegas bowl adds to the coolness factor - it's just so out of this world. It's definitely a game changer in the san diego area, and the possibilities are endless!

Writing this review just makes me want to go back - it is pretty pricey though. Depending on all your add-ons, you can easily spend $10.<//text>

< Text>
iDessert is a fancy made-to-order gelato dessert place created by famous chef Jean-Philippe.

You create your dessert with an ipad. You get to choose your meringue shell, gelato flavor, whether you want cake, fruit, and cream flavor. If you're feeling extra fancy and plan on instagramming your dessert, pay extra for the dry ice so you get that cool effect of a fog.

It looks cool, but I thought the dessert was okay. I wasn't a fan of the meringue shell. The gelato melted too fast. The dessert as a whole wasn't anything mindblowing. For me, it is a one time experience kind of place.

Place is small. They dont have enough tables. It sucks if the place is packed because this isn't the type of dessert that you can grab and eat while walking.</Text>
